 * =====================================================================================
 * EDGE
 * Search Group keyword: "edge"
 * 
 * edge browsers and rare formfactors
 * Old browsers
 * Low-use browsers
 * Browsers specialized for a specific purpose
 * Media players (audio and video)
 *
 * criteria: browser has active homepage
 * updates in last 5 years (after 2008)
 *
 * =====================================================================================
 
 * =====================================================================================
 * Browsers processed in common.txt
 * 
 * 
 * WebIE
 * Screenreader version of Internet Explorer
 * Screen presented in pure text
 * Interpreted as IE 6
 * http://www.webbie.org.uk/webbrowser/index.htm
 * 
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 * Baidu desktop
 * Early version of baidu browser, old IE Engine
 * http://finance.yahoo.com/news/chinas-baidu-releases-mobile-browser-033401013--finance.html
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 *
 * 
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 * Sleipnir browser
 * Japanese, customization and tab functions
 * superior text rendering onscreen 
 * IE clone
 * Mac, windows, iOS versions available
 * http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sleipnir_(web_browser)
 * IE9, IE8, IE7, IE6 trident engine
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 *
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 * Polarity
 * Web browser with multiple rendering engines (so in common.txt)
 * Old versions:
 * polarityweb.webs.com
 * New version:
 * polarityweb.weebly.com
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 *
 *
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 * Torch Browser
 * http://www.torchbrowser.com/
 * chromium based
 * download accelerator, torch music (can download instagram videos)
 * http://torchbrowser.codeplex.com/releases/view/105457
 * http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Torch_(web_browser)
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 *
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 * wkiosk/xstand - mac-based kiosk browser
 * recognized as Mac Safari
 * because there is no version number to match to the
 * release dates below in the user-agent
 *
 * Company formerly App4Mac, now ADNX in January 2012
 * wKiosk became xstand
 * 
 * http://www.xstandapp.com/en/index.html
 * versions:
 * http://www.xstandapp.com/en/index.html
 * 
 * wKiosk for Mac 6.x
 * similar to safari 5.0
 * May 12, 2010
 * wKiosk for Mac 5
 * wKiosk for Mac 4
 * June 17, 2005
 * wKiosk for Mac 3
 * December 1, 2003
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 *
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 * AvantBrowser
 * http://avantbrowser.com/
 * currently detected as msie
 * but has a tri-core so can appear as Chrome or Firefox
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 * 
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 * tenfourfox - firefox clone for powerpc macs
 * http://www.floodgap.com/software/tenfourfox/
 * http://code.google.com/p/tenfourfox/wiki/releasenotes1004
 * will run slow on older processors, but basically a FF clone, so don't break out
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 *
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 * SiteKiosk - secure public browsing based on IE
 * active since 2000, currently maintained
 * http://www.sitekiosk.com/en-US/Downloads/VersionHistory.aspx?Product=SiteKiosk
 * Since the same version of SiteKiosk may use different IE rendering engines,
 * detect at IE level
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 *
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 * Zac browser (interface for autistic children, no free surfing, uses Adobe Air
 * http://www.zacbrowser.com
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 * Xombrereo - security browser (2013)
 * Browser designed to be minimalist with lots of security features built in. 
 * http://opensource.conformal.com/wiki/xombrero
 *
 * =====================================================================================
 * Browsers processed in mobile.txt
 * =====================================================================================
 * 
 *
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 * Headless browsers (which almost always spoof, since they are part of unit 
 * testing or web apps
 * HTMLUnit
 * http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HtmlUnit
 * PhantomJS, CasperJS
 *
 * =====================================================================================
